function renderResults(results) {
  hideTile("tile-loading");

  renderVerdict(results);
  renderAssetBased(results);
  renderIncomeBased(results);
  renderMultiples(results);
  renderEnterprise(results);
  renderEquityMultiples(results);
  renderWACC(results);
  renderSummaryChart(results);
  renderDCFSensitivity(results);
}

function renderVerdict(results) {
  const profile = results.profile;
  const verdict = results.verdict;

  document.getElementById("val-company-name").textContent =
    `${profile.name} (${results.symbol})`;
  document.getElementById("val-company-meta").textContent =
    `${profile.sector || "—"} · ${profile.industry || "—"} · ${profile.exchange || "—"}`;
  document.getElementById("val-current-price").textContent =
    `$${profile.price.toFixed(2)}`;

  const badge = document.getElementById("val-verdict-badge");
  badge.textContent = verdict.rating;
  badge.className = "val-verdict-badge";
  if (verdict.score >= 60) badge.classList.add("undervalued");
  else if (verdict.score <= 40) badge.classList.add("overvalued");
  else badge.classList.add("fair");

  document.getElementById("val-fair-value").textContent = verdict.fairValue
    ? `$${verdict.fairValue.toFixed(2)}`
    : "N/A";
  document.getElementById("val-fair-range").textContent = verdict.range
    ? `$${verdict.range.low.toFixed(2)} — $${verdict.range.high.toFixed(2)}`
    : "N/A";

  // Meter
  const markerPos = Math.max(5, Math.min(95, verdict.score));
  document.getElementById("val-meter-marker").style.left = `${markerPos}%`;

  document.getElementById("val-data-provider").textContent =
    `Data from ${results.provider}`;

  showTile("tile-verdict");
}

function renderAssetBased(results) {
  const ab = results.valuations.assetBased;
  if (!ab) return;

  const metrics = [
    ["Book Value / Share", formatValuationCurrency(ab.bookValuePerShare)],
    ["Tangible Book / Share", formatValuationCurrency(ab.tangibleBookPerShare)],
    [
      "Liquidation Value / Share",
      formatValuationCurrency(ab.liquidationPerShare),
    ],
    ["Net-Net (NCAV) / Share", formatValuationCurrency(ab.ncavPerShare)],
    ["Tobin's Q", ab.tobinsQ ? formatRatio(ab.tobinsQ) : "N/A"],
    ["Replacement Cost", formatValuationCurrency(ab.replacementCost)],
  ];

  renderMetricList("val-asset-metrics", metrics);
  showTile("tile-asset");
}

function renderIncomeBased(results) {
  const ib = results.valuations.incomeBased;
  if (!ib) return;

  const metrics = [
    [
      "DCF Fair Value",
      formatValuationCurrency(ib.dcfPerShare),
      ib.dcfPerShare > 0,
    ],
    ["Graham Number", formatValuationCurrency(ib.grahamNumber)],
    ["Earnings Power Value", formatValuationCurrency(ib.epvPerShare)],
    ["Lynch Fair Value", formatValuationCurrency(ib.lynchFairValue)],
    ["Dividend Discount Model", formatValuationCurrency(ib.ddmValue)],
    ["FCF Growth Rate", formatPercent(ib.fcfGrowth)],
    ["Terminal Growth", formatPercent(ib.terminalGrowth)],
  ];

  renderMetricList("val-income-metrics", metrics);
  showTile("tile-income");
}

function renderMultiples(results) {
  const m = results.multiples;
  if (!m) return;

  const metrics = [
    ["P/E Ratio", formatRatio(m.peRatio)],
    ["Forward P/E", formatRatio(m.forwardPE)],
    [
      "PEG Ratio",
      formatRatio(m.pegRatio),
      m.pegRatio !== null ? m.pegRatio < 1 : null,
    ],
    ["Price / Sales", formatRatio(m.priceToSales)],
    ["Price / FCF", formatRatio(m.priceToFCF)],
    ["Earnings Growth", formatPercent(m.earningsGrowth)],
    ["Dividend Yield", formatPercent(m.dividendYield)],
  ];

  renderMetricList("val-multiples-metrics", metrics);
  showTile("tile-multiples");
}

function renderEnterprise(results) {
  const ev = results.enterprise;
  if (!ev) return;

  const metrics = [
    ["Enterprise Value", formatValuationCurrency(ev.enterpriseValue)],
    ["EV / EBITDA", formatRatio(ev.evToEbitda)],
    ["EV / Revenue", formatRatio(ev.evToRevenue)],
    ["EV / FCF", formatRatio(ev.evToFcf)],
    ["EV / Invested Capital", formatRatio(ev.evToInvestedCapital)],
    ["Invested Capital", formatValuationCurrency(ev.investedCapital)],
    ["ROIC", formatPercent(ev.roic)],
  ];

  renderMetricList("val-enterprise-metrics", metrics);
  showTile("tile-enterprise");
}

function renderEquityMultiples(results) {
  const m = results.multiples;
  const ab = results.valuations.assetBased;
  if (!m || !ab) return;

  const metrics = [
    ["Price / Book", formatRatio(m.priceToBook)],
    ["Price / Tangible Book", formatRatio(m.priceToTangibleBook)],
    [
      "Book Value Multiple",
      m.priceToBook ? formatRatio(m.priceToBook) + "x" : "N/A",
    ],
    ["Dividend Yield", formatPercent(m.dividendYield)],
    ["P/E Ratio", formatRatio(m.peRatio)],
    ["PEG Ratio", formatRatio(m.pegRatio)],
  ];

  renderMetricList("val-equity-metrics", metrics);
  showTile("tile-equity");
}

function renderWACC(results) {
  const ib = results.valuations.incomeBased;
  if (!ib) return;

  const metrics = [
    ["WACC", formatPercent(ib.wacc)],
    ["Cost of Equity", formatPercent(ib.costOfEquity)],
    [
      "Cost of Debt (after tax)",
      formatPercent(ib.costOfDebt * (1 - ib.taxRate)),
    ],
    ["Effective Tax Rate", formatPercent(ib.taxRate)],
    ["Risk-Free Rate", "4.3%"],
    ["Equity Risk Premium", "5.7%"],
    ["Dividend / Share", formatValuationCurrency(ib.dividendPerShare)],
  ];

  renderMetricList("val-wacc-metrics", metrics);
  showTile("tile-wacc");
}

function renderMetricList(containerId, metrics) {
  const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
  container.innerHTML = metrics
    .map(([label, value, isPositive]) => {
      let valueClass = "";
      if (isPositive === true) valueClass = "positive";
      else if (isPositive === false) valueClass = "negative";

      return `
      <div class="val-metric-row">
        <span class="val-metric-label">${label}</span>
        <span class="val-metric-value ${valueClass}">${value}</span>
      </div>
    `;
    })
    .join("");
}

// ===================================================================
// SUMMARY CHART
// ===================================================================

function renderSummaryChart(results) {
  const container = document.getElementById("val-summary-chart");
  const price = results.profile.price;
  const valuations = results.verdict.valuations;

  if (!valuations || valuations.length === 0) return;

  // Find the range for scaling
  const allValues = valuations.map((v) => v.value).concat([price]);
  const maxVal = Math.max(...allValues) * 1.2;

  const pricePercent = (price / maxVal) * 100;

  container.innerHTML = valuations
    .sort((a, b) => a.value - b.value)
    .map((v) => {
      const barPercent = Math.max(1, (v.value / maxVal) * 100);
      let barClass = "fair";
      if (v.value < price * 0.9) barClass = "over";
      else if (v.value > price * 1.1) barClass = "under";

      return `
        <div class="val-summary-row">
          <span class="val-summary-method">${v.method}</span>
          <div class="val-summary-bar-wrap">
            <div class="val-summary-bar ${barClass}" style="width: ${barPercent}%"></div>
            <div class="val-summary-price-line" style="left: ${pricePercent}%">
              <span class="val-summary-price-label">$${price.toFixed(0)}</span>
            </div>
          </div>
          <span class="val-summary-value">${formatValuationCurrency(v.value)}</span>
        </div>
      `;
    })
    .join("");

  showTile("tile-summary-chart");
}

// ===================================================================
// DCF SENSITIVITY TABLE
// ===================================================================

function renderDCFSensitivity(results) {
  const ib = results.valuations.incomeBased;
  const profile = results.profile;
  if (!ib || !ib.dcfPerShare || ib.dcfPerShare <= 0) return;

  const baseWACC = ib.wacc;
  const baseGrowth = ib.fcfGrowth;
  const shares = profile.sharesOutstanding;
  const balance = results.balance || [];
  const cashflow = results.cashflow || [];

  // Get base FCF and balance data
  const fcf = cashflow[0] ? cashflow[0].freeCashFlow : 0;
  const totalDebt = balance[0] ? balance[0].totalDebt : 0;
  const cash = balance[0] ? balance[0].cashAndEquivalents : 0;

  if (!fcf || !shares) return;

  // WACC variations: -2% to +2%
  const waccSteps = [-0.02, -0.01, 0, 0.01, 0.02];
  // Growth variations: -2% to +2%
  const growthSteps = [-0.02, -0.01, 0, 0.01, 0.02];

  const header = document.getElementById("val-dcf-sensitivity-header");
  const body = document.getElementById("val-dcf-sensitivity-body");

  // Header row
  header.innerHTML = `
    <tr>
      <th>WACC \\ Growth</th>
      ${growthSteps
        .map((gs) => {
          const g = baseGrowth + gs;
          const isCurrent = gs === 0;
          return `<th class="${isCurrent ? "current-col" : ""}">${(g * 100).toFixed(1)}%</th>`;
        })
        .join("")}
    </tr>
  `;

  // Body rows
  body.innerHTML = waccSteps
    .map((ws) => {
      const w = baseWACC + ws;
      const isCurrentRow = ws === 0;

      const cells = growthSteps
        .map((gs) => {
          const g = baseGrowth + gs;
          const isCurrentCol = gs === 0;
          const isCurrentCell = isCurrentRow && isCurrentCol;

          // Mini DCF calculation
          let dcfVal = 0;
          let projFCF = fcf;
          const termGrowth = 0.025;

          for (let t = 1; t <= 10; t++) {
            projFCF *= 1 + (t <= 5 ? g : g * 0.5);
            dcfVal += projFCF / Math.pow(1 + w, t);
          }

          if (w > termGrowth) {
            const tv = (projFCF * (1 + termGrowth)) / (w - termGrowth);
            dcfVal += tv / Math.pow(1 + w, 10);
          }

          dcfVal = (dcfVal - totalDebt + cash) / shares;

          let cellClass = "";
          if (isCurrentCell) cellClass = "current-cell";
          else if (isCurrentCol) cellClass = "current-col";
          else if (isCurrentRow) cellClass = "current-row";

          return `<td class="${cellClass}">${dcfVal > 0 ? "$" + dcfVal.toFixed(2) : "N/A"}</td>`;
        })
        .join("");

      return `
      <tr>
        <td class="${isCurrentRow ? "current-row" : ""}" style="font-weight: 600;">${(w * 100).toFixed(1)}%</td>
        ${cells}
      </tr>
    `;
    })
    .join("");

  showTile("tile-dcf-sensitivity");
}

// ===================================================================
// TILE VISIBILITY HELPERS
// ===================================================================

function showTile(id) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) el.classList.remove("hidden");
}

function hideTile(id) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) el.classList.add("hidden");
}

if (document.readyState === "loading") {
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", initValuator);
} else {
  initValuator();
}


============================================================
 FILE: /Users/careycarroll/Github Projects/financial-calculator/js/valuator.js

import { formatLargeNumberRaw, formatRatioPlain, formatPercent, formatValuationCurrency, calculateSimpleGrowthRates } from "./formatting.js";

// ===================================================================
// STOCK VALUATOR — Multi-Method Valuation Engine
// ===================================================================

export function evaluateStock(data) {
  const results = {
    symbol: data.symbol,
    provider: data.provider,
    profile: data.profile,
    valuations: {},
    multiples: {},
    enterprise: {},
    verdict: null,
  };

  const profile = data.profile;
  const income = data.income[0]; // Most recent year
  const balance = data.balance[0];
  const cashflow = data.cashflow[0];
  const prevIncome = data.income.length > 1 ? data.income : [];

  if (!profile || !income || !balance) {
    results.error = "Insufficient data for valuation";
    return results;
  }

  const price = profile.price;
  const shares = profile.sharesOutstanding || income.weightedAvgShares || 1;

  // =================================================================
  // ASSET-BASED VALUATION
  // =================================================================

  // Book Value
  const bookValue = balance.totalEquity;
  const bookValuePerShare = bookValue / shares;

  // Tangible Book Value
  const tangibleBook =
    bookValue - (balance.goodwill || 0) - (balance.intangibleAssets || 0);
  const tangibleBookPerShare = tangibleBook / shares;

  // Liquidation Value (conservative: current assets at 50%, fixed at 20%, minus all liabilities)
  const liquidationValue =
    (balance.totalCurrentAssets || 0) * 0.5 +
    (balance.propertyPlantEquipment || 0) * 0.2 +
    (balance.cashAndEquivalents || 0) * 1.0 -
    (balance.totalLiabilities || 0);
  const liquidationPerShare = liquidationValue / shares;

  // Net-Net (Graham's net current asset value)
  const ncav =
    (balance.totalCurrentAssets || 0) - (balance.totalLiabilities || 0);
  const ncavPerShare = ncav / shares;

  // Tobin's Q (Market Value / Replacement Cost approximation)
  const replacementCost =
    balance.totalAssets -
    (balance.goodwill || 0) -
    (balance.intangibleAssets || 0);
  const tobinsQ =
    replacementCost > 0 ? profile.marketCap / replacementCost : null;

  results.valuations.assetBased = {
    bookValue,
    bookValuePerShare,
    tangibleBook,
    tangibleBookPerShare,
    liquidationValue,
    liquidationPerShare,
    ncav,
    ncavPerShare,
    tobinsQ,
    replacementCost,
  };

  // =================================================================
  // INCOME-BASED VALUATION
  // =================================================================

  // WACC Calculation
  const totalDebt = balance.totalDebt || 0;
  const equity = profile.marketCap;
  const totalCapital = equity + totalDebt;
  const interestExpense =
    Math.abs(income.operatingIncome - income.ebitda) || totalDebt * 0.05;
  const costOfDebt = totalDebt > 0 ? interestExpense / totalDebt : 0.05;
  const taxRate =
    income.netIncome > 0 && income.operatingIncome > 0
      ? 1 - income.netIncome / income.operatingIncome
      : 0.21;
  const beta = profile.beta || 1.0;
  const riskFreeRate = 0.043; // ~10yr Treasury
  const marketReturn = 0.1; // Historical S&P avg
  const costOfEquity = riskFreeRate + beta * (marketReturn - riskFreeRate);
  const wacc =
    totalCapital > 0
      ? (equity / totalCapital) * costOfEquity +
        (totalDebt / totalCapital) * costOfDebt * (1 - taxRate)
      : costOfEquity;

  // DCF Valuation
  const fcf = cashflow ? cashflow.freeCashFlow : income.netIncome * 0.8;
  const growthRates = calculateSimpleGrowthRates(data.income);
  const revenueGrowth = growthRates.revenueGrowth || 0.05;
  const fcfGrowth = Math.min(revenueGrowth, 0.15); // Cap at 15%
  const terminalGrowth = 0.025; // Long-term GDP growth

  let dcfValue = 0;
  let projectedFCF = fcf;
  for (let t = 1; t <= 10; t++) {
    projectedFCF *= 1 + (t <= 5 ? fcfGrowth : fcfGrowth * 0.5);
    dcfValue += projectedFCF / Math.pow(1 + wacc, t);
  }
  // Terminal value
  const terminalValue =
    (projectedFCF * (1 + terminalGrowth)) / (wacc - terminalGrowth);
  dcfValue += terminalValue / Math.pow(1 + wacc, 10);
  // Subtract debt, add cash
  dcfValue = dcfValue - totalDebt + (balance.cashAndEquivalents || 0);
  const dcfPerShare = dcfValue / shares;

  // Graham Number
  const eps = income.eps || income.netIncome / shares;
  const grahamNumber =
    eps > 0 && bookValuePerShare > 0
      ? Math.sqrt(22.5 * eps * bookValuePerShare)
      : null;

  // Earnings Power Value (no growth assumed)
  const adjustedEarnings = income.ebitda
    ? income.ebitda * (1 - taxRate)
    : income.netIncome;
  const epv = wacc > 0 ? adjustedEarnings / wacc : null;
  const epvPerShare = epv
    ? (epv - totalDebt + (balance.cashAndEquivalents || 0)) / shares
    : null;

  // Peter Lynch Fair Value (PEG-based)
  const earningsGrowth =
    growthRates.epsGrowth || growthRates.netIncomeGrowth || 0.05;
  const lynchFairPE = Math.max(earningsGrowth * 100, 5); // Growth rate as fair P/E
  const lynchFairValue = eps > 0 ? eps * lynchFairPE : null;

  // Dividend Discount Model
  const dividendsPaid = cashflow ? Math.abs(cashflow.dividendsPaid || 0) : 0;
  const dividendPerShare = dividendsPaid / shares;
  const dividendGrowth = Math.min(earningsGrowth, 0.08);
  const ddmValue =
    dividendPerShare > 0 && costOfEquity > dividendGrowth
      ? (dividendPerShare * (1 + dividendGrowth)) /
        (costOfEquity - dividendGrowth)
      : null;

  results.valuations.incomeBased = {
    wacc,
    costOfEquity,
    costOfDebt,
    taxRate,
    dcfValue,
    dcfPerShare,
    fcfGrowth,
    terminalGrowth,
    grahamNumber,
    epv,
    epvPerShare,
    lynchFairValue,
    lynchFairPE,
    ddmValue,
    dividendPerShare,
  };

  // =================================================================
  // MARKET MULTIPLES
  // =================================================================

  const peRatio = eps > 0 ? price / eps : null;
  const forwardPE =
    earningsGrowth > 0 && eps > 0 ? price / (eps * (1 + earningsGrowth)) : null;
  const pegRatio =
    peRatio && earningsGrowth > 0 ? peRatio / (earningsGrowth * 100) : null;
  const priceToBook = bookValuePerShare > 0 ? price / bookValuePerShare : null;
  const priceToTangibleBook =
    tangibleBookPerShare > 0 ? price / tangibleBookPerShare : null;
  const priceToSales =
    income.revenue > 0 ? profile.marketCap / income.revenue : null;
  const priceToFCF = fcf > 0 ? profile.marketCap / fcf : null;
  const dividendYield = dividendPerShare > 0 ? dividendPerShare / price : 0;

  results.multiples = {
    peRatio,
    forwardPE,
    pegRatio,
    priceToBook,
    priceToTangibleBook,
    priceToSales,
    priceToFCF,
    dividendYield,
    earningsGrowth,
  };

  // =================================================================
  // ENTERPRISE VALUE
  // =================================================================

  const enterpriseValue =
    profile.marketCap + totalDebt - (balance.cashAndEquivalents || 0);
  const evToEbitda = income.ebitda > 0 ? enterpriseValue / income.ebitda : null;
  const evToRevenue =
    income.revenue > 0 ? enterpriseValue / income.revenue : null;
  const evToFcf = fcf > 0 ? enterpriseValue / fcf : null;
  const investedCapital =
    balance.totalEquity + totalDebt - (balance.cashAndEquivalents || 0);
  const evToInvestedCapital =
    investedCapital > 0 ? enterpriseValue / investedCapital : null;
  const roic =
    investedCapital > 0
      ? (income.operatingIncome * (1 - taxRate)) / investedCapital
      : null;

  results.enterprise = {
    enterpriseValue,
    evToEbitda,
    evToRevenue,
    evToFcf,
    evToInvestedCapital,
    investedCapital,
    roic,
  };

  // =================================================================
  // VERDICT
  // =================================================================

  results.verdict = calculateVerdict(price, results);

  return results;
}

// ===================================================================
// GROWTH RATE CALCULATIONS
// ===================================================================

// calculateSimpleGrowthRates imported from formatting.js

// ===================================================================
// VERDICT ENGINE
// ===================================================================

export function calculateVerdict(price, results) {
  const valuations = [];

  // Collect all per-share valuations
  const ab = results.valuations.assetBased;
  const ib = results.valuations.incomeBased;

  if (ab.bookValuePerShare > 0)
    valuations.push({
      method: "Book Value",
      value: ab.bookValuePerShare,
      weight: 0.5,
    });
  if (ab.tangibleBookPerShare > 0)
    valuations.push({
      method: "Tangible Book",
      value: ab.tangibleBookPerShare,
      weight: 0.5,
    });
  if (ab.liquidationPerShare)
    valuations.push({
      method: "Liquidation Value",
      value: ab.liquidationPerShare,
      weight: 0.3,
    });
  if (ab.ncavPerShare > 0)
    valuations.push({
      method: "Net-Net (NCAV)",
      value: ab.ncavPerShare,
      weight: 0.3,
    });
  if (ib.dcfPerShare > 0)
    valuations.push({ method: "DCF", value: ib.dcfPerShare, weight: 1.5 });
  if (ib.grahamNumber > 0)
    valuations.push({
      method: "Graham Number",
      value: ib.grahamNumber,
      weight: 1.0,
    });
  if (ib.epvPerShare > 0)
    valuations.push({
      method: "Earnings Power Value",
      value: ib.epvPerShare,
      weight: 1.0,
    });
  if (ib.lynchFairValue > 0)
    valuations.push({
      method: "Lynch Fair Value",
      value: ib.lynchFairValue,
      weight: 0.8,
    });
  if (ib.ddmValue > 0)
    valuations.push({
      method: "Dividend Discount",
      value: ib.ddmValue,
      weight: 0.6,
    });

  if (valuations.length === 0) {
    return {
      rating: "Insufficient Data",
      score: 50,
      fairValue: null,
      range: null,
      valuations: [],
    };
  }

  // Weighted average fair value
  const totalWeight = valuations.reduce((sum, v) => sum + v.weight, 0);
  const weightedFairValue =
    valuations.reduce((sum, v) => sum + v.value * v.weight, 0) / totalWeight;

  // Fair value range (25th to 75th percentile of estimates)
  const sorted = valuations.map((v) => v.value).sort((a, b) => a - b);
  const low = sorted[Math.floor(sorted.length * 0.25)];
  const high = sorted[Math.floor(sorted.length * 0.75)];

  // Score: 0 = extremely overvalued, 50 = fair, 100 = extremely undervalued
  const ratio = weightedFairValue / price;
  const score = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(ratio * 50)));

  let rating;
  if (score >= 75) rating = "Significantly Undervalued";
  else if (score >= 60) rating = "Undervalued";
  else if (score >= 45) rating = "Fairly Valued";
  else if (score >= 30) rating = "Overvalued";
  else rating = "Significantly Overvalued";

  return {
    rating,
    score,
    fairValue: weightedFairValue,
    range: { low, high },
    valuations,
  };
}

// ===================================================================
// FORMATTING HELPERS
// ===================================================================

// Formatting functions imported from formatting.js

              💡 How This Works <span class="cm-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
            </button>
            <div class="cm-explainer-body hidden" id="sp-explainer-body">
              <p><strong>Contribution Margin (CM)</strong> is the amount left over after subtracting variable costs from revenue. It contributes first to covering fixed costs, then to profit.</p>
              <p><strong>Gross Profit (GP)</strong> subtracts only COGS (cost of goods sold) from revenue. The difference: CM uses all variable costs; GP uses only production-related costs you designate as COGS.</p>
              <p><strong>Breakeven</strong> is the point where total revenue equals total costs — operating income is exactly $0. Below breakeven you lose money; above it you profit.</p>
              <p><strong>Margin of Safety</strong> is how far your actual (or target) volume is above breakeven — expressed as a percentage. Higher is safer.</p>
              <p><strong>Known Volume mode</strong> — enter how many units you sold or plan to sell. The tool calculates actual operating income and shows where you stand relative to breakeven.</p>
              <p><strong>Target Profit mode</strong> — enter a profit goal (or $0 for breakeven). The tool solves for how many units you need to sell to hit that target.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Product Setup</h2>

            <!-- Mode Toggle -->
            <div class="mode-toggle" style="margin-bottom:1.25rem;">

              <button id="sp-mode-target" class="btn-toggle">🎯 Target Profit</button>

              </button>
              <div class="cm-explainer-body hidden" id="vc-explainer-body">
                <p><strong>Variable costs</strong> change in direct proportion to the number of units produced or sold. Common examples:</p>
                <ul>
                  <li><strong>Direct Materials</strong> — raw materials used to make each unit</li>
                  <li><strong>Direct Labor</strong> — wages paid per unit produced</li>
                  <li><strong>Variable Manufacturing Overhead</strong> — utilities, supplies that vary with production</li>
                  <li><strong>Variable Selling Costs</strong> — commissions, shipping per unit sold</li>
                </ul>
                <p>Check <strong>COGS</strong> for costs that are part of the cost of goods sold (production costs). Leave unchecked for variable selling/admin costs. This determines Gross Profit vs Contribution Margin.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Add each variable cost line item. Check "COGS" if it should be included in Gross Profit calculation.</p>
            <div id="sp-variable-costs" class="cost-list"></div>

          <!-- Fixed Costs -->
          <div class="calc-form">

            <div class="cm-explainer">
              <button class="cm-explainer-toggle" id="fc-explainer-toggle" aria-expanded="false">
                💡 What are fixed costs? <span class="cm-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
              </button>
              <div class="cm-explainer-body hidden" id="fc-explainer-body">
                <p><strong>Fixed costs</strong> remain constant regardless of how many units you produce or sell. Common examples:</p>
                <ul>
                  <li><strong>Rent / Lease</strong> — facility costs that don't change with volume</li>
                  <li><strong>Salaries</strong> — management and administrative staff</li>
                  <li><strong>Depreciation</strong> — equipment and asset depreciation</li>
                  <li><strong>Insurance</strong> — fixed premiums</li>
                  <li><strong>Fixed Overhead</strong> — any production overhead that doesn't vary with output</li>
                </ul>
                <p>Fixed costs are what the contribution margin must first cover before any profit is generated. The breakeven point is where CM exactly equals total fixed costs.</p>
              </div>

        <!-- ==================== TAB 2: MULTI-PRODUCT ==================== -->
        <div id="multi-tab" class="hidden">

          <!-- How This Works -->
          <div class="cm-explainer">
            <button class="cm-explainer-toggle" id="mp-explainer-toggle" aria-expanded="false">
              💡 How Multi-Product Analysis Works <span class="cm-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
            </button>
            <div class="cm-explainer-body hidden" id="mp-explainer-body">
              <p><strong>Sales Mix</strong> is the proportion of each product in total sales. If you sell 600 units of Product A and 400 of Product B, the mix is 60%/40%. Mix percentages must sum to 100%.</p>
              <p><strong>Weighted Average CM</strong> blends each product's CM per unit by its sales mix. This single number represents the average contribution of one "bundle" unit sold.</p>
              <p><strong>Bundle Breakeven</strong> is the total number of units (across all products) needed to cover fixed costs, assuming the sales mix holds constant.</p>
              <p><strong>Breakeven Option A</strong> allocates fixed costs to each product by its mix percentage, then solves for that product's individual units. Each product "pays its share" of fixed costs.</p>
              <p><strong>Breakeven Option B</strong> solves for total bundle units first, then multiplies by each product's mix. This is the standard managerial accounting approach.</p>
              <p><strong>Capacity Constraint</strong> — when a shared resource (machine hours, labor hours) is limited, you should prioritize products with the highest CM per unit of that resource — not just the highest CM per unit. This is the Theory of Constraints.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Products -->
          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Products</h2>
            <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Add each product. Sales mix % must sum to 100%.</p>
            <div id="mp-products" class="mp-product-list"></div>
            <button id="mp-add-product" class="btn-secondary" style="margin-top:1rem;">+ Add Product</button>
          </div>

            <button id="mp-add-fixed" class="btn-add" style="margin-top:0.75rem;">+ Add Fixed Cost</button>

                <input type="checkbox" id="mp-constraint-toggle" />
                <span class="toggle-slider"></span>
              </label>
            </div>
            <p class="form-hint">Enable to rank products by CM per unit of constrained resource (e.g. machine hours, labor hours).</p>
            <div id="mp-constraint-fields" class="conditional-fields hidden">
              <div class="form-row">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="mp-resource-name">Resource Name</label>
                  <input type="text" id="mp-resource-name" placeholder="e.g. Machine Hours" />
                </div>
                <div class="form-group">

            <div class="cm-explainer">
              <button class="cm-explainer-toggle" id="sens-explainer-toggle" aria-expanded="false">
                💡 How Sensitivity Analysis Works <span class="cm-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
              </button>
              <div class="cm-explainer-body hidden" id="sens-explainer-body">
                <p><strong>Sensitivity analysis</strong> shows how your results change when key assumptions change. This is critical for decision-making under uncertainty.</p>
                <p><strong>Price sensitivity</strong> — a small price increase often has a large impact on CM because variable costs don't change. This is called <em>operating leverage</em>.</p>
                <p><strong>Volume sensitivity</strong> — shows how much volume needs to change to hit breakeven or a profit target. Useful for sales planning.</p>
                <p><strong>Variable cost sensitivity</strong> — models the impact of input cost changes (materials, labor). If your supplier raises prices, how does that affect your breakeven?</p>
                <p><strong>Fixed cost sensitivity</strong> — models the impact of adding capacity, hiring staff, or signing a new lease.</p>
                <p>The <strong>sensitivity matrix</strong> shows operating income at every combination of price and volume adjustments simultaneously — giving you a full picture of the risk/reward landscape.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1.5rem;">Adjust sliders to see how changes affect contribution margin, breakeven, and operating income. Based on Single Product inputs — calculate that tab first.</p>

            <div id="sensitivity-no-data" class="cm-flag" style="display:block;">
              ⚠️ Calculate the Single Product tab first to enable sensitivity analysis.
            </div>

            <div id="sensitivity-controls" class="hidden">
              <div class="sensitivity-slider-group">
                <label>Price Adjustment: <span id="sens-price-label" class="sens-value">0%</span></label>
                <input type="range" id="sens-price" class="sens-slider" min="-30" max="30" value="0" step="1" />
                <div class="sens-range-labels"><span>-30%</span><span>+30%</span></div>
              </div>
              <div class="sensitivity-slider-group">

                <div class="sens-range-labels"><span>-50%</span><span>+50%</span></div>
              </div>
              <div class="sensitivity-slider-group">

                <input type="range" id="sens-vc" class="sens-slider" min="-30" max="30" value="0" step="1" />
                <div class="sens-range-labels"><span>-30%</span><span>+30%</span></div>

      <header>
        <h1>📐 Consumer Theory</h1>
        <p class="tagline">Price elasticity, cross-price effects, expected utility, and risk premium — interactive tools for economics.</p>
      </header>

      <main>
        <div class="ct-tabs">
          <button id="tab-elasticity" class="ct-tab active" aria-label="Price elasticity tab">📐 Price Elasticity</button>
          <button id="tab-cross-price" class="ct-tab" aria-label="Cross-price elasticity tab">🔗 Cross-Price</button>
          <button id="tab-eu" class="ct-tab" aria-label="Expected utility tab">🎲 Expected Utility</button>
          <button id="tab-risk-premium" class="ct-tab" aria-label="Risk premium tab">💰 Risk Premium</button>

        <!-- ==================== TAB 1: PRICE ELASTICITY ==================== -->
        <div id="elasticity-tab">

          <div class="ct-explainer">
            <button class="ct-explainer-toggle" id="elas-explainer-toggle" aria-expanded="false">
              💡 How Price Elasticity Works <span class="ct-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
            </button>
            <div class="ct-explainer-body hidden" id="elas-explainer-body">
              <p><strong>Price elasticity of demand (ε)</strong> measures how responsive quantity demanded is to a change in price. It answers: if price rises by 1%, how much does quantity fall?</p>
              <p>The formula is: <strong>ε = (∂q/∂p) × (p/q)</strong>. Because demand slopes downward, ε is always negative for demand.</p>
              <p><strong>Elastic demand (|ε| &gt; 1):</strong> quantity is very sensitive to price. A price increase causes revenue to fall because the quantity drop outweighs the price gain.</p>
              <p><strong>Inelastic demand (|ε| &lt; 1):</strong> quantity is not very sensitive to price. A price increase causes revenue to rise because the price gain outweighs the quantity drop.</p>
              <p><strong>Unit elastic (|ε| = 1):</strong> revenue is unchanged for a small price change.</p>
              <p><strong>From Equation mode</strong> solves for equilibrium P* and Q* first, then computes elasticity at that point — exactly like the lecture worked example.</p>
              <p><strong>Solve for P or Q</strong> lets you work backwards: given a target elasticity, find the price or quantity where that elasticity holds.</p>
              <p><strong>Arc elasticity</strong> uses the midpoint formula between two observed data points.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Input Method</h2>
            <div class="mode-toggle" style="margin-bottom:1.25rem; flex-wrap:wrap; gap:0.5rem;">
              <button id="elas-mode-equation" class="btn-toggle active">📋 From Equation</button>
              <button id="elas-mode-point" class="btn-toggle">📐 Find ε</button>
              <button id="elas-mode-solve" class="btn-toggle">🎯 Solve for P or Q</button>
              <button id="elas-mode-arc" class="btn-toggle">📍 Arc Elasticity</button>
            </div>

            <!-- From Equation Inputs -->
            <div id="elas-equation-inputs">
              <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Enter your demand and supply equations. The tool solves for equilibrium P* and Q*, then computes elasticity at that point.</p>
              <div class="micro-curve-inputs" style="display:grid; grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr; gap:1.5rem; margin-bottom:1.25rem;">
                <div class="micro-curve-block demand" style="background:var(--bg-primary); border:1px solid var(--border); border-left:3px solid #f472b6; border-radius:10px; padding:1.25rem;">
                  <h3 style="font-size:0.95rem; font-weight:700; color:#f472b6; margin-bottom:0.75rem;">📉 Demand Curve</h3>
                  <div class="form-group">
                    <label for="elas-eq-d-const">Constant (a)</label>
                    <input type="number" id="elas-eq-d-const" placeholder="e.g. 16" step="any" />
                    <span class="form-hint">q = a + b·P  →  enter a</span>
                  </div>
                  <div class="form-group">
                    <label for="elas-eq-d-coef">Price Coefficient (b)</label>
                    <input type="number" id="elas-eq-d-coef" placeholder="e.g. -2" step="any" />
                    <span class="form-hint">Negative for downward-sloping demand</span>
                  </div>
                  <div id="elas-eq-demand-preview" style="margin-top:0.75rem; padding:0.6rem 1rem; background:var(--bg-secondary); border:1px solid var(--border); border-radius:6px; font-family:monospace; font-size:0.9rem; color:var(--accent);">q = a + b·P</div>
                </div>
                <div class="micro-curve-block supply" style="background:var(--bg-primary); border:1px solid var(--border); border-left:3px solid #2dd4bf; border-radius:10px; padding:1.25rem;">
                  <h3 style="font-size:0.95rem; font-weight:700; color:#2dd4bf; margin-bottom:0.75rem;">📈 Supply Curve</h3>
                  <div class="form-group">
                    <label for="elas-eq-s-const">Constant (c)</label>
                    <input type="number" id="elas-eq-s-const" placeholder="e.g. -2" step="any" />
                    <span class="form-hint">q = c + d·P  →  enter c</span>
                  </div>
                  <div class="form-group">
                    <label for="elas-eq-s-coef">Price Coefficient (d)</label>
                    <input type="number" id="elas-eq-s-coef" placeholder="e.g. 1" step="any" />
                    <span class="form-hint">Positive for upward-sloping supply</span>
                  </div>
                  <div id="elas-eq-supply-preview" style="margin-top:0.75rem; padding:0.6rem 1rem; background:var(--bg-secondary); border:1px solid var(--border); border-radius:6px; font-family:monospace; font-size:0.9rem; color:var(--accent);">q = c + d·P</div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Find ε Inputs -->
            <div id="elas-point-inputs" class="hidden">
              <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Enter the slope of your equation and the price/quantity at the point of interest.</p>
              <div class="form-row">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-curve-type">Curve Type</label>
                  <select id="elas-curve-type">
                    <option value="demand">Demand</option>
                    <option value="supply">Supply</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-dqdp">∂q/∂p (slope of curve)</label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-dqdp" placeholder="e.g. -2 for demand, 1 for supply" step="any" />
                  <span class="form-hint">The coefficient on P in your equation.</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div class="form-row">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-p">Price (P)</label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-p" placeholder="e.g. 6" step="any" min="0" />
                </div>
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-q">Quantity (Q)</label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-q" placeholder="e.g. 4" step="any" min="0" />
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Solve for P or Q Inputs -->
            <div id="elas-solve-inputs" class="hidden">
              <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Enter a target elasticity and two of the three variables — the tool solves for the third.</p>
              <div class="mode-toggle" style="margin-bottom:1.25rem;">
                <button id="elas-solve-q-btn" class="btn-toggle active">Solve for Q</button>
                <button id="elas-solve-p-btn" class="btn-toggle">Solve for P</button>
              </div>
              <div class="form-row">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-solve-curve-type">Curve Type</label>
                  <select id="elas-solve-curve-type">
                    <option value="demand">Demand</option>
                    <option value="supply">Supply</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-solve-eps">Target Elasticity (ε)</label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-solve-eps" placeholder="e.g. -2 or 1.5" step="any" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <div class="form-row">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-solve-dqdp">∂q/∂p (slope)</label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-solve-dqdp" placeholder="e.g. -2" step="any" />
                </div>
                <div class="form-group" id="elas-solve-p-group">
                  <label for="elas-solve-p">Price (P) <span style="color:var(--accent);">← known</span></label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-solve-p" placeholder="e.g. 6" step="any" min="0" />
                  <span class="form-hint">Solving for Q at this price.</span>
                </div>
                <div class="form-group hidden" id="elas-solve-q-group">
                  <label for="elas-solve-q">Quantity (Q) <span style="color:var(--accent);">← known</span></label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-solve-q" placeholder="e.g. 4" step="any" min="0" />
                  <span class="form-hint">Solving for P at this quantity.</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Arc Elasticity Inputs -->
            <div id="elas-arc-inputs" class="hidden">
              <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Enter two observed price-quantity pairs. The arc elasticity uses the midpoint formula.</p>
              <div class="form-row">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-arc-curve-type">Curve Type</label>
                  <select id="elas-arc-curve-type">
                    <option value="demand">Demand</option>
                    <option value="supply">Supply</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
                <div class="form-group"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="form-row">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-p1">Price 1 (P₁)</label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-p1" placeholder="e.g. 5" step="any" min="0" />
                </div>
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label for="elas-q1">Quantity 1 (Q₁)</label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-q1" placeholder="e.g. 10" step="any" min="0" />
                </div>

                </div>

                  <label for="elas-q2">Quantity 2 (Q₂)</label>
                  <input type="number" id="elas-q2" placeholder="e.g. 6" step="any" min="0" />
                </div>

            </div>

            <button id="elas-calculate" class="btn-primary">Calculate Elasticity</button>

            <div class="results-grid results-grid-3">
              <div class="result-item">
                <span class="result-label">Price Elasticity (ε)</span>

            </div>

          <!-- Step-by-Step -->
          <div id="elas-steps-section" class="hidden" style="margin-bottom:2rem;">
            <div class="ct-explainer" style="border-color: var(--accent);">
              <button class="ct-explainer-toggle" id="elas-steps-toggle" aria-expanded="true">
                🧮 Step-by-Step Calculation <span class="ct-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
              </button>
              <div class="ct-explainer-body" id="elas-steps-body">
                <div id="elas-steps-content" class="ct-steps-content"></div>

          <!-- Chart -->
          <div id="elas-chart-section" class="chart-panel hidden">
            <h2>Elasticity Diagram</h2>
            <div class="canvas-chart">
              <canvas id="elas-chart-canvas" role="img" aria-label="Price elasticity diagram showing demand curve with elastic and inelastic regions"></canvas>
            </div>
          </div>

        </div>

        <!-- ==================== TAB 2: CROSS-PRICE ELASTICITY ==================== -->
        <div id="cross-price-tab" class="hidden">

          <div class="ct-explainer">
            <button class="ct-explainer-toggle" id="cross-explainer-toggle" aria-expanded="false">
              💡 How Cross-Price Elasticity Works <span class="ct-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
            </button>
            <div class="ct-explainer-body hidden" id="cross-explainer-body">
              <p><strong>Cross-price elasticity</strong> measures how the quantity demanded of Good i responds to a change in the price of Good j.</p>
              <p><strong>Substitutes (ε &gt; 0):</strong> when the price of Good j rises, consumers buy more of Good i instead. Example: Pepsi and Coke.</p>
              <p><strong>Complements (ε &lt; 0):</strong> when the price of Good j rises, consumers buy less of Good i too. Example: cars and gasoline.</p>
              <p><strong>Independent (ε ≈ 0):</strong> the price of Good j has no meaningful effect on demand for Good i.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Cross-Price Elasticity</h2>
            <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Enter two observations of Good i's quantity at different prices of Good j.</p>
            <div class="form-row">
              <div class="form-group">
                <label for="cross-good-i">Good i Name (optional)</label>
                <input type="text" id="cross-good-i" placeholder="e.g. Pepsi" />
              </div>
              <div class="form-group">
                <label for="cross-good-j">Good j Name (optional)</label>
                <input type="text" id="cross-good-j" placeholder="e.g. Coke" />
              </div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-row">
              <div class="form-group">
                <label for="cross-pj1">Price of Good j — Point 1 (Pⱼ₁)</label>
                <input type="number" id="cross-pj1" placeholder="e.g. 2.00" step="any" min="0" />
              </div>
              <div class="form-group">
                <label for="cross-qi1">Quantity of Good i — Point 1 (Qᵢ₁)</label>
                <input type="number" id="cross-qi1" placeholder="e.g. 100" step="any" min="0" />
              </div>
            </div>
            <div class="form-row">
              <div class="form-group">
                <label for="cross-pj2">Price of Good j — Point 2 (Pⱼ₂)</label>
                <input type="number" id="cross-pj2" placeholder="e.g. 2.50" step="any" min="0" />
              </div>
              <div class="form-group">
                <label for="cross-qi2">Quantity of Good i — Point 2 (Qᵢ₂)</label>

            <h2>Cross-Price Relationship</h2>
            <div class="canvas-chart">
              <canvas id="cross-chart-canvas" role="img" aria-label="Cross-price elasticity chart showing relationship between Good j price and Good i quantity"></canvas>
            </div>

        <!-- ==================== TAB 3: EXPECTED UTILITY ==================== -->
        <div id="eu-tab" class="hidden">

          <div class="ct-explainer">
            <button class="ct-explainer-toggle" id="eu-explainer-toggle" aria-expanded="false">
              💡 How Expected Utility Works <span class="ct-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
            </button>
            <div class="ct-explainer-body hidden" id="eu-explainer-body">
              <p><strong>Expected utility</strong> is not the same as expected payoff. When consumers are risk-averse, they have diminishing marginal utility of wealth — each additional dollar is worth less than the last.</p>
              <p><strong>Expected Payoff</strong> = Σ (probability × payoff). This is just the probability-weighted average outcome.</p>
              <p><strong>Expected Utility</strong> = Σ (probability × u(payoff)). This applies the utility function first, then takes the weighted average.</p>
              <p>Because of diminishing marginal utility, a risk-averse person prefers a certain $1M over a 50/50 shot at $2M — even though both have the same expected payoff. The utility function captures this preference.</p>
              <p>The utility function you choose determines how risk-averse the agent is: <strong>√x</strong> and <strong>ln(x)</strong> are concave (risk-averse), <strong>x</strong> is linear (risk-neutral), and <strong>x²</strong> is convex (risk-seeking).</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Utility Function</h2>
            <div class="ct-utility-selector" id="eu-utility-selector">
              <button class="ct-utility-btn active" data-fn="sqrt">u(x) = √x</button>
              <button class="ct-utility-btn" data-fn="log">u(x) = ln(x)</button>
              <button class="ct-utility-btn" data-fn="linear">u(x) = x</button>
              <button class="ct-utility-btn" data-fn="square">u(x) = x²</button>
            </div>
            <p class="form-hint">Units are in thousands ($). Enter payoffs as numbers (e.g. 100 = $100,000).</p>
          </div>

          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Options</h2>
            <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Add up to 3 options. Each option can have up to 4 outcomes. Probabilities must sum to 1.0 per option.</p>
            <div id="eu-options-list"></div>
            <button id="eu-add-option" class="btn-secondary" style="margin-top:0.75rem;">+ Add Option</button>
          </div>

          <button id="eu-calculate" class="btn-primary">Calculate Expected Utility</button>

          <!-- Results -->
          <div id="eu-results" class="results-panel hidden" aria-live="polite">
            <h2>Expected Utility Results</h2>

              </div>

              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

              <button class="ct-explainer-toggle" id="eu-steps-toggle" aria-expanded="true">

            <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Each option's outcomes are plotted on the utility curve. The gap between expected payoff and expected utility illustrates risk aversion.</p>
            <div class="canvas-chart">
              <canvas id="eu-chart-canvas" role="img" aria-label="Utility curve showing expected utility vs expected payoff for each option"></canvas>
            </div>
          </div>

        </div>

        <!-- ==================== TAB 4: RISK PREMIUM ==================== -->
        <div id="risk-premium-tab" class="hidden">

          <div class="ct-explainer">
            <button class="ct-explainer-toggle" id="rp-explainer-toggle" aria-expanded="false">
              💡 How Risk Premium Works <span class="ct-explainer-chevron">▼</span>
            </button>
            <div class="ct-explainer-body hidden" id="rp-explainer-body">
              <p><strong>Risk premium</strong> is how much of the expected payoff you would give up to eliminate all uncertainty. It measures the cost of risk to a risk-averse agent.</p>
              <p><strong>Certainty Equivalent (CE)</strong> is the guaranteed amount that gives you the same utility as the risky investment. If CE = $80K and the expected payoff is $100K, you'd accept $80K for certain rather than take the gamble.</p>
              <p><strong>Risk Premium = Expected Payoff − Certainty Equivalent.</strong> In the example above, the risk premium is $20K — that's how much you'd pay to eliminate the risk.</p>
              <p><strong>Willingness to Pay (WTP)</strong> is the maximum you'd pay today for the risky asset, equal to the present value of the certainty equivalent (ignoring discount rates here, WTP = CE).</p>
              <p>The larger the risk premium, the more risk-averse the agent. A risk-neutral agent has a risk premium of zero.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Utility Function</h2>
            <div class="ct-utility-selector" id="rp-utility-selector">
              <button class="ct-utility-btn active" data-fn="sqrt">u(x) = √x</button>
              <button class="ct-utility-btn" data-fn="log">u(x) = ln(x)</button>
              <button class="ct-utility-btn" data-fn="linear">u(x) = x</button>
              <button class="ct-utility-btn" data-fn="square">u(x) = x²</button>
            </div>
            <p class="form-hint">Units are in thousands ($). Enter payoffs as numbers (e.g. 100 = $100,000).</p>
          </div>

          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Risky Asset</h2>
            <p class="form-hint" style="margin-bottom:1rem;">Enter the possible outcomes and their probabilities. Probabilities must sum to 1.0.</p>
            <div id="rp-outcomes-list"></div>
            <button id="rp-add-outcome" class="btn-secondary" style="margin-top:0.75rem;">+ Add Outcome</button>
          </div>

          <button id="rp-calculate" class="btn-primary">Calculate Risk Premium</button>

          <!-- Results -->
          <div id="rp-results" class="results-panel hidden" aria-live="polite">
            <h2>Risk Premium Results</h2>
            <div class="results-grid results-grid-3">
              <div class="result-item">

              </div>

              </div>

<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>Supply & Demand | Financial Calculator</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/base.css" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/common-calculator.css" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/micro-econ.css" />
  </head>
  <body>
    <nav class="top-nav">
      <div class="top-nav-inner">
        <a href="../index.html" class="top-nav-logo">Financial Calculator</a>
        <div class="top-nav-links">
          <a href="../index.html" class="top-nav-link active">Calculators</a>
          <a href="news.html" class="top-nav-link">News Feed</a>
        </div>
      </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="page-container">
      <header>
        <h1>📉 Supply & Demand</h1>
        <p class="tagline">Define linear supply and demand curves, solve for market equilibrium, and explore how shifts affect the market.</p>
      </header>

      <main>
        <!-- Tab Navigation -->
        <div class="micro-tabs">
          <button id="tab-equilibrium" class="micro-tab active" aria-label="Market equilibrium tab">⚖️ Equilibrium</button>
          <button id="tab-shifters" class="micro-tab" aria-label="Curve shifters tab">🎛️ Curve Shifters</button>
        </div>

        <!-- ==================== TAB 1: EQUILIBRIUM ==================== -->
        <div id="equilibrium-tab">

          <!-- Input Mode Toggle -->
          <div class="calc-form">
            <h2 class="form-section-title">Input Method</h2>
            <div class="mode-toggle" style="margin-bottom:1.25rem;">
              <button id="mode-equation" class="btn-toggle active">𝑓(x) Equation</button>
              <button id="mode-points" class="btn-toggle">📍 Two Points</button>
